For people that don't understand how the one guy was D3, the biggest thing to notice is that though he was playing slower and doing a few awkward things, it was a short clip. It could have just been one of those times where you just lose that flow and feel. That said, watch his patience and positioning. He never took himself out of the play, the times he committed to anything was when it was safe, he was there to make that save and only really fucked up because he came in too close to the back wall and hit the transition, something EVERYONE does from time to time. Dude literally started the clip with a good challenge that almost lead to a goal had it gone a little more on net. He then challenged again leading the defender to lose possession giving his teammate a good shot opportunity. He didn't over commit on it, kept control of his car, etc. Awkwardness starts after that, but a lot of that is stuff that really would have been fine had they been a bit more on.
